(function($){
// Vars
	var d = $(document),
		w = $(window),
		vport = w.width(),
		b = $('body'),
		f = $('footer.footer'),

	/* Below should match variables from _variables.less */
		// screenXs = 240,
		// screenSm = 480,
		screenMd = 768,
		screenLg = 992,
		screenXl = 1200,
		//screenXsMax = (screenSm - 1),
		//screenSmMax = (screenMd - 1),
		//screenMdMax = (screenLg - 1),
		//screenLgMax = (screenLg + 20),


	/* modal vars */
		modal,
		mClasses,


	/* dResize Var */
		resizeTimer;





// Functions
	/*
	* Function for delayed resize
	* USE:  w.dResize(function(){});
	*/
	$.fn.dResize = function(data, fn){
		return arguments.length > 0 ?
			this.on('delayed-resize', null, data, fn):
			this.trigger('dResize');
	};

	$.Velocity.RegisterEffect('fadeInPanels', {
	  defaultDuration: 500,
	  calls: [
	    [{
	      opacity: [1, 0.3],
	      scale: [1, 0.5]
	    }]
	  ]
	});

	$('.panel').velocity('fadeInPanels', {
	  stagger: 250,
	});




	// Modal Content switcher
	var modalSwitcher = function(modal, mTrigger, mTitle, mContent){
		if(modal.find('.modal-pager')){
			modal.find('.modal-pager .modal-pager-button').off('click');
		}

		mClasses = mTrigger.attr('data-modal-classes');

		modal.find('.modal-dialog').addClass(mClasses);
		modal.find('.modal-header .modal-title').html(mTitle);
		modal.find('.modal-body').html(mContent);

		if(modal.find('.modal-pager')){
			modal.find('.modal-pager .modal-pager-button').click(function(){
				var nmTrigger;

				if($(this).hasClass('prev')){
					nmTrigger = mTrigger.parent().prev().length ? mTrigger.parent().prev().find('.modal-trigger') : mTrigger.parent().parent().children().last().find('.modal-trigger');
				}else{
					nmTrigger = mTrigger.parent().next().length ? mTrigger.parent().next().find('.modal-trigger') : mTrigger.parent().parent().children().first().find('.modal-trigger');
				}

				var nmTitle = nmTrigger.find(nmTrigger.attr('data-modal-title-holder')).html(),
					nmContent = nmTrigger.find(nmTrigger.attr('data-modal-content-holder')).html();

				modalSwitcher(modal, nmTrigger, nmTitle, nmContent);
			});
		}
	};

		/* Primary menu RElated - bc no .container (class name) element wraps this */
	  	function distanceLeft() {
	  		var distance = $('.menu-toggle-icon').offset();
	  		var distanceFromLeft = distance.left,
	  			bfl = distanceFromLeft + 380, // bkgd from left
	  			//ffl = distanceFromLeft + 440, // fade from left
	  			mfl = distanceFromLeft + 3; //menu from left
	  			$('.primary-menu-bkgd').css('max-width',bfl);
	  			$('.primary-menu-wrap').css('left',mfl);
	  			$('.hero .vertical-shade').css('max-width',bfl);
	  	}


	  	function lifeWorkPos() {
	  		var distanceMenu = $('.menu-toggle-icon').offset(),
	  			leftEdge = distanceMenu.left + 3;
	  		var distanceSearch = $('.search-toggle-icon'),
	  			rightEdge = ( w.width() - ( distanceSearch.offset().left + distanceSearch.outerWidth() ) );
  			/* homepage */
  			if ( vport > screenLg) {
  				$('.his-work').velocity({
  				    left: leftEdge,
  				}, {
  				    duration: 1250,
  				    delay: 500
  				});
  				$('.his-life').velocity({
  				    right: rightEdge,
  				}, {
  				    duration: 1250,
  				    delay: 500
  				});
  			} else {
  				$('.his-work').css('left',leftEdge);
  				$('.his-life').css('right',rightEdge);
  			}
	  	}

	  	function lifeWorkRePos() {
	  		var distanceMenu = $('.menu-toggle-icon').offset(),
	  			leftEdge = distanceMenu.left + 3;
	  		var distanceSearch = $('.search-toggle-icon'),
	  			rightEdge = ( w.width() - ( distanceSearch.offset().left + distanceSearch.outerWidth() ) );
	  			/* homepage */
	  			$('.his-work').css('left',leftEdge);
	  			$('.his-life').css('right',rightEdge);
	  	}

	  	var menuIs = 'closed',
	  		lmu = $('.block-artglass-main-menu ul.menu'),
	  		lmi = $('.block-artglass-main-menu ul.menu li.menu-item');

	 	function toggleNav() {
	 		distanceLeft();
	 		b.toggleClass('disable-scroll');

	 		$('.canvas-bkgd').toggleClass('active');
	 		$('.menu-toggle-icon').toggleClass('open');
	 		$('.primary-menu-bkgd').toggleClass('active');
	 		$('.primary-menu-wrap').toggleClass('active');
	 		$('header.header').toggleClass('inactive');
	 		$('.site-name').toggleClass('hidden');
	 		$('.search-toggle-icon').toggleClass('hidden');

	 		if ( menuIs === 'closed') {
	 			menuIs = 'open';
	 			$('.menu-toggle-text').text('close');
	 		} else {
	 			menuIs = 'closed';
	 			$('.menu-toggle-text').text('menu');
	 		}

	 		$(lmu).velocity("fadeIn", { duration: 1000 });
	 		$(lmi).velocity("slideDown", { duration: 500 });
	 		//$(this).blur(
	 	}

	 	function closeNav() {
	 		b.removeClass('disable-scroll');
	 		menuIs = 'closed';
 			$('.menu-toggle-text').text('menu');
			$('.canvas-bkgd.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.primary-menu-bkgd.active, .primary-menu.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.menu-toggle-icon.open').removeClass('open');
			$('.primary-menu-wrap').removeClass('active');
			$('header.header.inactive').removeClass('inactive');
			$('.site-name.hidden').removeClass('hidden');
			$('.search-toggle-icon.hidden').removeClass('hidden');
		}
		function toggleSearch() {
			b.toggleClass('disable-scroll');
			$('.canvas-bkgd').toggleClass('active');
			$('.icon-search.search-toggle-icon').toggleClass('hidden');
			$('.search-bkgd').toggleClass('active');
			$('.menu-toggle-wrap').toggleClass('hidden');
			$('header.header').toggleClass('inactive');
			$('.block-artglass-search').toggleClass('active');
			$('.site-name').toggleClass('hidden');
			$(this).blur();
		}
		function closeSearch() {
			b.removeClass('disable-scroll');
			$('.canvas-bkgd').removeClass('active');
			$('.search-bkgd.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.icon-search.search-toggle-icon.hidden').removeClass('hidden');
			$('.menu-toggle-wrap.hidden').removeClass('hidden');
			$('header.header.inactive').removeClass('inactive');
			$('.block-artglass-search.active').removeClass('active');
			$('.site-name.hidden').removeClass('hidden');
		}

		function fullVideo() {
			var e, t, i, o, n, vbh;
			var winWidth = w.width(),
				winHeight = w.height();

			if ( $("#video-bg video").length ) {
				e = $("#video-bg video").attr("width");
				t = $("#video-bg video").attr("height");
			}

			if ( winHeight / winWidth > t / e ) {
				i = winHeight / t * e;
				o = winHeight;
				n = -(i - winWidth) / 2;
				$("#video-bg").css("width", i).css("height", o).css("top", "0").css("bottom", "0").css("left", n).css("right", "auto");
				vbh = $('#video-bg').height();
				$(".no-video-bg").css("height", vbh);
			} else {
				i = winWidth;
				o = winWidth * (t / e);
				n = -(o - winHeight) / 2;
				$("#video-bg").css("width", i).css("height", o).css("top", n).css("bottom", "auto").css("left", "0").css("right", "0");
				vbh = $('#video-bg').height();
				$(".no-video-bg").css("height", vbh);
			}

		}

		function modalReposition() {
	        var modal = $(this),
	            dialog = modal.find('.modal-dialog');
	        modal.css('display', 'block');
	        // Dividing by two centers the modal exactly, but dividing by three
	        // or four works better for larger screens.
	        dialog.css("margin-top", Math.max(0, ($(window).height() - dialog.height()) / 2));
	    }


	    function heroIntro() {
	    	$('.hero-curtain').velocity({
	    		opacity: 0
	    	}, {
	    	    delay: 1000,
	    	    duration: 250
	    	});
	    	$('.hero-curtain').hide();
	    	$('h2.field-display-title').velocity({
	    		opacity: 1,
	    		left: "0px"
	    	},{
	    	    delay: 1250,
	    	    duration: 250
	    	});
	    	$('#work-series-intro-arrow').velocity({
	    		bottom: "120px"
	    	},{
	    		delay: 250,
	    		duration: 250
	    	});
	    }

	    function workNavPosition() {
	    	/* initialize Bootstrap scrollspy */
	    	$('body').scrollspy({ target: '#block-views-block-work-block-2' });
	    	/* set vars for dynamic affix position */
	    	var heroHeight = $('.intro.hero.full-height').height(),
	    		heroHeightxHalf = heroHeight + ( heroHeight / 2 );
	    	/* position block in the middle of the second section */
	    	$('#block-views-block-work-block-2').css('top',heroHeightxHalf);
	    	/* initialize Bootstrap Affix w/ offset */
	    	$('#block-views-block-work-block-2').affix({
	    		offset: {
	    	    	top: heroHeight,
	    	    	bottom: ( heroHeight / 2 ) + 50

	    	  	}
	    	});
	    }

	    function lifeNav() {
	    	var heroHeight = $('#page-hero-intro').height();
	    	$('.life-menu-wrap').affix({
	    		offset: {
	    	    	top: heroHeight
	    	  	}
	    	});
	    	/* handles browser resize < lg to >= xl, iPad Pro orientation change*/
	    	if ( vport > screenXl ) {
	    			//console.log('xl screen');
	    			$('#spacebar').removeClass('open');
	    			//
	    			$('#menu-life-resources').hide();
	    			//
	    			$('#life-canvas-cover').removeClass('active');
	    			$('.life-menu-wrap').show();

	    	} else {
	    			//console.log('less than xl screen');
	    			$('#spacebar').removeClass('open');
	    			$('ul#more-resources > li.open').removeClass('open');
	    			$('.life-menu-wrap').hide();
	    			$('#menu-life-resources').show();

	    	}
	    }

	    function activeLife() {
	    	var whatsActive = $('.chihuly-tabs a.active').text();
	    	$('#spacebar span').html(whatsActive);
	    }


		function imageCover(){
			$('.paragraph--type--two-column-images').each( function() {
				var items = $(this).find('.image-wrap'),
					checkHeight = 0;

				if($(window).width() > screenMd){ // Use $(window) instead of w so that is checks the new size of the window
					items.each(function(){
						$(this).css({'min-height' : 0}).removeClass('short tall'); // unset styles and remove classes
						checkHeight = $(this).height() > checkHeight ? $(this).height() : checkHeight;
					});

					items.each(function(){
						// Action to do for shorter or taller...
						// Use CSS to adjust the image wrapper height
						// Use class name enable the BG image and hide the FG image
						if($(this).height() < checkHeight){
							$(this).css({'min-height' : checkHeight}).addClass('short');
						}else{
							$(this).addClass('tall');
						}
					});
				}else{
					items.css({'min-height' : 0}).removeClass('short').addClass('tall'); // unset styles and remove classes
				}
			});
		}




// Actions
	b.removeClass('no-js');
	$('html').addClass('js');

	// Helper action to fire delayed resize
	w.resize(function(e){
		clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
		resizeTimer = setTimeout(function(){
			w.trigger('delayed-resize', e);
		}, 250);
	});


	/*
	// Hide Header on on scroll down
	var didScroll;
	var lastScrollTop = 0;
	var delta = 1;
	var navbarHeight = $('header.header').outerHeight();

	setInterval(function() {
	    if (didScroll) {
	        hasScrolled();
	        didScroll = false;
	    }
	}, 250);

	function hasScrolled() {
	    var st = $(this).scrollTop();

	    // Make sure they scroll more than delta
	    if(Math.abs(lastScrollTop - st) <= delta) {
	    	return;
	    }

	    // If they scrolled down and are past the navbar, add class .nav-up.
	    // This is necessary so you never see what is "behind" the navbar.
	    if (st > lastScrollTop && st > navbarHeight){
	        // Scroll Down
	        b.addClass('hide-header');
	    } else {
	        // Scroll Up
	        if(st + $(window).height() < $(document).height()) {
	            b.removeClass('hide-header');
	        }
	    }

	    lastScrollTop = st;
	}
	*/



	d.ready(function(){

		/* Main Menu Left Edge */
		distanceLeft();

		/* Homepage */
		fullVideo();
		lifeWorkPos();

		/* fade from black */
		heroIntro();

		/* Front page, left-side */
		$('.intro-block.his-work .wrap').on('mouseenter', function() {
			if ( vport > screenLg) {

				$('.pan-lr .pan-bkgd')
          .css('width',vport)
          .css('left', Math.abs(parseInt($('#video-bg').css('left'))));

    			/* bkgd image slides left to display */
    			$('.pan-mask.pan-lr').velocity({
    			    width: "100%"
    			}, {
    			    duration: 250
    			});
    			/* button slides down */
    			$('.his-work .field').velocity({
    			    height: '100%',
    			    translateY: '10px'
    			}, {
    			    duration: 250,
    			    delay: 250,
    			    display: 'block',
    			    easing: "ease"
    			});
	    		/* fade opposing link */
	    		$('.his-life a.h2').toggleClass('faded');
		    }
    	});
		$('.intro-block.his-work .wrap').on('mouseleave', function() {
			if ( vport > screenLg) {
				/* button slides up and no display */
				$('.his-work .field').velocity({
				    height: '0%',
				    translateY: '-10px'
				}, {
				    duration: 250,
				    delay: 0,
				    display: 'none',
				    easing: "ease"
				});
				/* bkgd image slides right to hide */
				$('.pan-mask.pan-lr').velocity({
				    width: "0%"
				}, {
					delay: 250,
				    duration: 250
				});
	    		/* reveal opposing link */
	    		$('.his-life a.h2').toggleClass('faded');
		    }
    	});

		/* Front page, right-side */
    	$('.intro-block.his-life .wrap').on('mouseenter', function() {
			if ( vport > screenLg) {

				$('.pan-rl .pan-bkgd')
          .css('width',vport)
          .css('left', Math.abs(parseInt($('#video-bg').css('left'))));

    			/* bkgd image slides left to display */
    			$('.pan-mask.pan-rl').velocity({
    			    width: "100%"
    			}, {
    			    duration: 250
    			});
    			/* button slides down */
    			$('.his-life .field').velocity({
    			    height: '100%',
    			    translateY: '10px'
    			}, {
    			    duration: 250,
    			    delay: 250,
    			    display: 'block',
    			    easing: "ease"
    			});
	    		/* fade opposing link */
	    		$('.his-work a.h2').toggleClass('faded');
		    }
    	});
		$('.intro-block.his-life .wrap').on('mouseleave', function() {
			if ( vport > screenLg) {
				/* button slides up and no display */
				$('.his-life .field').velocity({
				    height: '0%',
				    translateY: '-10px'
				}, {
				    duration: 250,
				    delay: 0,
				    display: 'none',
				    easing: "ease"
				});
				/* bkgd image slides right to hide */
				$('.pan-mask.pan-rl').velocity({
				    width: "0%"
				}, {
					delay: 250,
				    duration: 250
				});
	    		/* reveal opposing link */
	    		$('.his-work a.h2').toggleClass('faded');
		    }
    	});


		/* Scroll To Anchor when href="" #id */
		/* For example, "back to top" link, or .intro-arrow scroll down */
		if (!$('body').hasClass("life-timeline")) {

			$('a[href*=\\#]').click(function(e) {
				var u = this.hash,
	            t = $(u),
	            i = t.offset().top;
			    e.preventDefault();
			    $('html,body').velocity("scroll", {
			    	duration: 1000,
			    	offset: i + 'px'
			    });
			});

		}


		/* Bootstrap Tooltip -- once initialized here, data attribute handles click & focus events */
		$('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();


		/* Modal Position vertical Center */
		$('.modal').on('show.bs.modal', modalReposition);

		// #dynamic-modal content process (from Bearbase)
		$('#dynamic-modal').on('show.bs.modal', function(e){
			var mTrigger = $(e.relatedTarget),
				mTitle = mTrigger.find(mTrigger.attr('data-modal-title-holder')).html(),
				mContent = mTrigger.find(mTrigger.attr('data-modal-content-holder')).html();

			modal = $(this);

			modalSwitcher(modal, mTrigger, mTitle, mContent);
		}).on('hide.bs.modal', function(){
			modal.find('.modal-dialog').removeClass(mClasses);
			if(modal.find('.modal-pager')){
				modal.find('.modal-pager .modal-pager-button').off('click');
			}
			modal.find('.modal-header .modal-title').html('');
			modal.find('.modal-body').html('');

			mClasses = '';
		});

		/* don't navigate away anchor tag */
	    $('.no-link').on('click', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
		});

		/* Modal Trigger Image Enlarge */
	    $('.image-toggle-icon').on('click', function() {
			/* which image we lookin at? */
			//var imgSRC = $(this).prev().find('img').attr('src');
			var imgSRC = $(this).parent(".image-wrap").clone(),
				imgCaption = $(this).parent().next(".image-caption").clone(),
				inquireTF = $(this).data('inquire-link'),
				heroInstance = $(this).data('hero'),
				bkgdColor = $(this).data('bkgd-color'),
				inquireLink = $('.inquire-explore-links').clone();
			/* Hero section is different markup -- the source image is a background-image. The caption has different relativity in the markup */
			if ( heroInstance === true ) {
				imgSRC = $(this).parent('#work-series-hero-intro').css('background-image');
				imgSRC = imgSRC.replace('url(','').replace(')','').replace(/\"/gi, "");
				imgSRC = '<div class="image-wrap ' + bkgdColor + '"><img src="' + imgSRC + '" class="modal-img" /></div>';
				if ( $('.work-series-caption').length ) {
					imgCaption = $(this).prev('.work-series-caption').html();
					imgCaption = '<div class="image-caption">'+ imgCaption +'</div>' ;
				}
			}
			/* put image in the modal */
			$('#artglassModal .modal-body').prepend(imgSRC);
			// this line in conjunction with imageCover();
			$('#artglassModal .modal-body .image-wrap').css('background-image','none');
			/* get the caption ready.. */
			$('#artglassModal .modal-body').append(imgCaption);
			/* if inquire-link is TRUE */
			if ( inquireTF === true ) {
				$('#artglassModal .modal-body').append(inquireLink);
				/* cloned element contains tooltip that needs to be initialized */
				$('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
			}
			/* now, show the modal */
			$('#artglassModal').modal('show');

			/* Now, when it's closed... */
			$('#artglassModal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
			  /* remove the content we added */
			  $('.modal-body').empty();
			});
		});

		/* Video In Modal */
		$('.video-trigger').on('click', function() {

			var	videoSRC = $(this).prev().clone();

			/* put image in the modal */
			//$('#artglassModal .modal-body').prepend('<div class="image-wrap"><img src="' + imgSRC + '" class="modal-img" /></div>');
			$('#artglassModal .modal-body').prepend(videoSRC);

			$('#artglassModal .modal-dialog').addClass('video-inside');

			/* now, show the modal */
			$('#artglassModal').modal('show');

			/* Now, when it's closed... */
			$('#artglassModal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
			  $('#artglassModal .modal-dialog').removeClass('video-inside');
			  /* remove the content we added */
			  $('.modal-body').empty();
			});
		});

		/* css-tricks responsive iframe for YT & Vimeo - JS necessary to detect aspect ratio, doesn't assume 16:9 */
		// Find all YouTube videos
		var $allVideos = $("iframe[src^='//player.vimeo.com'], iframe[src^='//www.youtube.com']"),
			// The element that is fluid width
		    $fluidEl = $("body");
		// Figure out and save aspect ratio for each video
		$allVideos.each(function() {
		  $(this)
		    .data('aspectRatio', this.height / this.width)
		    // and remove the hard coded width/height
		    .removeAttr('height')
		    .removeAttr('width');
		});
		// When the window is resized
		$(window).resize(function() {
		  var newWidth = $fluidEl.width();
		  // Resize all videos according to their own aspect ratio
		  $allVideos.each(function() {
		    var $el = $(this);
		    $el
		      .width(newWidth)
		      .height(newWidth * $el.data('aspectRatio'));
		  });
		// Kick off one resize to fix all videos on page load
		}).resize();


		/* His Work Page Views Block Text Links Secondary Nav*/
		if ( $('#block-views-block-work-block-2').length ) {
			workNavPosition();
		}

		if ( $('.paragraph--type--two-column-images').length ) {
			imageCover();
		}

		// Sticky Footer; but not on <front> where it animates in
		if (!$('body').hasClass("path-frontpage")) {
			var footerHeight = $('footer.footer').height();
			b.css('margin-bottom',footerHeight);
			f.css('height',footerHeight);
		}


		w.on('resize', function() {

		  clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
		  resizeTimer = setTimeout(function() {
		    // Run code here, resizing has "stopped"

			vport = w.width();

		    distanceLeft();

		    fullVideo();

		    lifeWorkRePos();

		    $('.modal:visible').each(modalReposition);

		    // Sticky Footer re-sized
		    if (!$('body').hasClass("path-frontpage")) {
		    	// this removes the previously set height, lets it flow to natural height
		    	$('footer.footer').css('height', 'auto');
				// ok, now measure again.
		    	var newfooterHeight = $('footer.footer').height();
				b.css('margin-bottom',newfooterHeight);
				f.css('height',newfooterHeight);
			}


		    /* His Work Page Views Block Text Links Secondary Nav*/
		    if ( $('#block-views-block-work-block-2').length ) {
		    	/* supports the dynamic affix position */
		    	$(window).off('.affix');
		    	$('#block-views-block-work-block-2').removeData('bs.affix').removeClass('affix affix-top affix-bottom');
				/* call function again, as in document ready */
		    	workNavPosition();
		    }
		    /* His Life */
		    if ( $('#life-header-menus').length ) {
		    	lifeNav();
		    }

			if ( $('.paragraph--type--two-column-images').length ) {
				imageCover();
			}

		    // Grid customizations dev log
			/*var winWidth = w.width(),
				conWidth = $('.grid-test.container').width();
			console.log(
				'window width: ' + winWidth + '\n' +
				'container width: ' + conWidth
			);	*/
		  }, 0);
		});


		/* Timeline Accordion */

		/* clean up this field for consistency -- no apostrophe or quote in the string */
		$('.bkgd-year').each( function() {
			var yearVal = $(this).text().replace('\'','').replace('"','');
			$(this).text(yearVal);
		});

		/* open the first item */
		$("#timelineAccordion").find('.timeline-item:first .collapse').collapse('show');

		/* initialize */
		$('.field--name-field-timeline-facets-and-events').slick({
			nextArrow: '<i class="fa fa-angle-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
			prevArrow: '<i class="fa fa-angle-left" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
			responsive: true,
			dots: true,
			customPaging: function(slider, i) {
			    // label each dot with relative year (slide value)
			    return '<button class="tab gravy">' + $(slider.$slides[i]).find('.teaser-date').text() + '</button>';
			  },
		});

		/* data-parent attribute doesn't work due to the nested markup  */
	    $('#timelineAccordion a[data-toggle=collapse]').on('click', function() {
	    	/* this click function will hide the open ones */
			$('#timelineAccordion').find('.collapse.in').collapse('hide');

			$(this).parent().parent().parent().addClass('timeline-faded');

			$('#timelineAccordion ').on('shown.bs.collapse','.collapse', function() {
				$(this).find('.field--name-field-timeline-facets-and-events').slick('setPosition');
				$('.timeline-faded').removeClass('timeline-faded');
			});

			$('#timelineAccordion ').on('hidden.bs.collapse','.collapse', function() {
				$(this).find('.field--name-field-timeline-facets-and-events').slick('slickGoTo',0);
			});

		});



		$('.menu-toggle-wrap').click(function(){
			toggleNav();
		});
		$('.canvas-bkgd').click(function(){
			closeNav();
			closeSearch();
		});

		$('.search-toggle-icon').click(function(){
			toggleSearch();
		});

		$('.block-artglass-search input[type=search]').attr('placeholder','Search');



	    // Menu as Tabs
	    if ($('.chihuly-tabs').length) {
	      var $menuTabs = $('.chihuly-tabs');
	      var $articles = $menuTabs.parents('article').find('article');
	      // Ignore child articles (e.g. node teasers from view)
	      $articles = $articles.not($articles.find('article'));

	      $articles.hide();

	      // Add anchors to menu
	      $menuTabs.find('a').each(function(i, el) {
	        if ($(el).attr('href').indexOf('#') === -1) {
	          $(el).attr('href', '#' + $(el).attr('href'));
	        }
	      });

	      $menuTabs.find('a').click(function() {
	        $('#block-life a').removeClass('active');
	        $(this).addClass('active');

	        $articles.hide();

	        var href = $(this).attr('href').replace('#', '');
	        $('article[about="' + href + '"]').show();

	        /* Initialize Slick Carousel on Exhibition Teaser */
	        /* on /exhibitions, past-exhibitions is hidden until tab is clicked */
			var $pastTab = $('article[about="/past-exhibitions"]');
			var $pastTabLink = $('a[href="#/past-exhibitions"]');
			/* can't initialize js on a hidden element, wait until it's visible */
			if ( ($pastTab.is(':visible')) && (!$pastTabLink.hasClass('initialized')) ) {
				$('.field--name-field-exhibition-slideshow').slick({
					nextArrow: '<i class="fa fa-angle-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
					prevArrow: '<i class="fa fa-angle-left" aria-hidden="true"></i>',
					dots: true
				});
				/* flag the link as clicked, so to only initialize once */
				$pastTabLink.addClass('initialized');
			}

	      });

	      // Set active tab based on hash
	      if (document.location.hash) {
	      	/* there's #/ in the URL, go to that item */
	        $('a[href="' + document.location.hash + '"]').click();
	      } else {
	      	/* no #/ in the URL, go to the first menu item */
	        $menuTabs.find('a').eq(0).click();
	      }

	      /* mobile/tablet element (#spacebar) which menu-item is a.active */
	      activeLife();

	    }

		if($('.chihuly-tab').length && $('.chihuly-tabs').length){
			var $tab = $('.chihuly-tab'),
				$tabs = $('.chihuly-tabs'),
				$tabArticles = $tabs.parents('article').find('article');

			// Ignore child articles (e.g. node teasers from view)
			$tabArticles = $tabArticles.not($tabArticles.find('article'));

			// Add anchors to menu
			$tab.find('a').each(function(i, el){
				if($(el).attr('href').indexOf('#') === -1){
					$(el).attr('href', '#' + $(el).attr('href'));
				}
			});

			$tab.find('a').click(function(e){
				e.preventDefault();
				var href = $(this).attr('href').replace('#', '');
				$tabs.find('a:eq('+$tabArticles.index($('article[about="' + href + '"]'))+')').click();
			});
		}

	    if ( $('#life-header-menus').length ) {
	    	lifeNav();
	    }

	    /* Life Landing Page  */
	    $('#menu-life .menu-item a').on('click', function(e) {
	    	$('#menu-life .menu-item a').removeClass('active');
	    	$(this).addClass('active');
	    	activeLife();
	    	/* close dropdown */
	    	if ( vport < screenLg ) {
				$('#spacebar').toggleClass('open');
			  	var slideDir = $('.life-menu-wrap').is(':visible') ? 'slideUp' : 'slideDown';
			  	$('.life-menu-wrap').velocity(slideDir);
			  	$('#life-canvas-cover').toggleClass('active');
	    	}


	    	/* scroll to top --  */
	    	var it = $('.views-element-container').offset().top;
	        e.preventDefault();
	        $('html,body').velocity("scroll", {
	        	duration: 1000,
	        	offset: it + 'px'
	        });

	    });


    	/* exhibitions landing page */
    	/* Very similar to Life click function above; however the source markup differs */
        $('ul#menu-exhib li a').on('click', function(e) {

        	$('ul#menu-exhib li a').removeClass('active');
        	$(this).addClass('active');
        	activeLife();
        	/* close dropdown */
        	if ( vport < screenLg ) {
    			$('#spacebar').toggleClass('open');
    		  	var slideDir = $('.life-menu-wrap').is(':visible') ? 'slideUp' : 'slideDown';
    		  	$('.life-menu-wrap').velocity(slideDir);
    		  	$('#life-canvas-cover').toggleClass('active');
        	}

        	/* scroll to top --  */
        	var it = $('.tab-content:visible .views-element-container').offset().top;
            e.preventDefault();
            $('html,body').velocity("scroll", {
            	duration: 1000,
            	offset: it + 'px'
            });

        });



	    /* More Resources Dropdown */
	    $('ul#more-resources > li > a.more').on('click', function(e) {
	    	// don't navigate away
	    	e.preventDefault();
	    	// add class for bkgd color
	    	$(this).parent().toggleClass('open');
	    	// slide the drawer
	      	var slideDir = $('#menu-life-resources').is(':visible') ? 'slideUp' : 'slideDown';
	      	$('#menu-life-resources').velocity(slideDir);
	    });

	    /* Life Menu Mobile/Tablet -  */
	    $('#spacebar').on('click', function() {
	    	// add class for bkgd color
	    	$(this).toggleClass('open');
	      	var slideDir = $('.life-menu-wrap').is(':visible') ? 'slideUp' : 'slideDown';
	      	$('.life-menu-wrap').velocity(slideDir);
	      	$('#life-canvas-cover').toggleClass('active');
	    });

	    $('#life-canvas-cover').on('click',function() {
	    		$('#spacebar').toggleClass('open');
	    	  	var slideDir = $('.life-menu-wrap').is(':visible') ? 'slideUp' : 'slideDown';
	    	  	$('.life-menu-wrap').velocity(slideDir);
	    	  	$('#life-canvas-cover').removeClass('active');
	    });


	    /* Exhibit Date */
	    if ( $('.page-node-type-exhibition').length ) {
	    	/* assist in the formatting of php date. Trims year from start date. For example: JUL 1 - NOV 30, 1985 */
	    	var targetDate = $('.field--name-field-exhib-dates time:first').text();
		    targetDate = targetDate.slice(0, -6);
		    $('.field--name-field-exhib-dates time:first').text(targetDate);
	    }


		w.load(function(){
			// Display Chihuly Loader on page load
			if(vport > screenLg){
				if($('.chihuly-loader').length){
					$('.chihuly-loader').velocity({
						delay: 1000,
						duration: 3000,
						backgroundColorAlpha: 0
					});
					$('.chihuly-loader').velocity("fadeOut", {
						delay: 1000,
						duration: 500
					});
					$('header.header').velocity("fadeIn", {
						delay: 1500,
						duration: 250
					});
					$('footer.footer').velocity("slideDown", {
						delay: 1500,
						duration: 250
					});
				}
			}
		});

	});

  // Used for Ajax view forms
  Drupal.behaviors.autosubmit = {
    attach: function() {  // Function options - context, settings
      $('.form-autosubmit :input').change(function() {
        $(this.form).find('.form-submit').click();
      });


    }
  };


})(jQuery);
